 Budhia Singh, who achieved the reputation of becoming the youngest marathon runner in the world by running 65 km without stopping at the age of just four years, is living in the darkness of oblivion today
 apni uplabdhi se sabhi ko hairaan karne vaale 'vander kid' budhiya par bani hindi film 'duranto' ko 63wein rashtriya film puraskaar main sarvshereshth bal film puraskaar se nawaja gaya
 In the recent past, Budhia came into the limelight only with this film
 uski asal pahchaan jis cheez ke liye he, vah usase dur hota ja rahaa he
 In 2006, Budhia, who crossed the 65-km journey from Puri to Bhubaneshwar in seven hours and two minutes, made a place in the 'limca Book of Records', but today he is living an anonymous life in the streets of Odisha
 'duranto' film main darshaya gaya ki kaise mahaj chaar saal kaa baccha ek sitara ban gaya or phir achaanak gir kar kahin gum ho gaya
 Born in 2002 in a poor Odisha family, Budhia was sold by her mother to a person for just Rs 800
 iske baad judo-karate ke ek coach biranchi das ne use god le liya
 Biranchi crafted Budhia by training her talent to become a marathon runner
 unke hi maargdarshan kaa nateeja tha ki chaar varsh kii umr main usne itnaa bada karishma kar dikhaaya
 Budhia's training for marathon running did not go well with the Odisha government's child welfare department and they banned it and sent it to the sports hostel in Bhubaneswar
 haalanki, vah ab bhi olympic padak jeetne kaa icchhuk he
 Budhia told IANS, "I need a personal coach to fulfill my dream
 main marathon ke liye prashikshan mil rahaa tha, lekin mujhe 100-200 meter kii daud ke liye prashikshit kiya ja rahaa he
 " chandrashekharpur ke diavi vidhyalay main aathvin kaksha ke chaatr budhiya ne kaha ki use apni padhai puri kerani he or isliye vah keval ek ghante abhyaas karata he
 Her mother Sukanti Singh also has a complaint against the sports administration of the state government
 sukanti ne ieenes ko bataaya, "mere bete ke liye khel chatravaas main poshak bhojan nahin he
 He repeatedly complains to me that he should not stay in the hostel
 agar koi mere bete ko prashikshan de, to main ise chatravaas chhodane ke liye kahuungi
 " adhikariyon ne haalanki, in sabhi aalochanaon kaa khandan kiya

 Chennai Super Kings team opener Murali Vijay has become the first Indian batsman to score two centuries in the Indian Premier League (IPL)
 ipel main teen shatak lagane vaale kris gail ekmaatr ballebaaj hai jabaki do shatak adam gilcrist ke naam bhi he
 Vijay achieved this feat against Delhi Daredevils in the second qualifier match played on Friday under the fifth edition of the IPL
 unhone 51 gendon par shatak lagaaya
 During this, he hit 13 fours and four sixes
 maujuuda sanskaran main shatak lagane vaale vijay chathe ballebaaj hai
 Earlier in the season, Rajasthan Royals opener Ajinkya Rahane (103 not out), Delhi Daredevils' Kevin Pietersen (103 not out) and David Warner (109 not out), Rohit Sharma (109 not out) and Chris Gayle (128 not out) scored centuries

 vijay kaa ipel main yah doosraa shatak he
 Earlier, he scored a century against Rajastha Royals in the third edition of IPL
 is match main unhone sirf 56 gendon par 127 ran thonk die the
 Among the Indian players in the IPL, Manish Pandey, Yusuf Pathan, Paul Walthaty, Sachin Tendulkar, Virender Sehwag, Rahane and Rohit have each scored a century each
 ipel main kisi bhartiya khilaadi dwaara pehla shatak lagane kaa ricard royal chalangers bangalore ke khilaadi pandeya ke naam rahaa he
 Pandey scored his first century in the second edition of the 2009 IPL against Deccan Chargers
 unhone 73 gendon par 114 ranon kii pari kheli thi
 During this, he hit 10 fours and four sixes
 ipel main sabase tej shatak lagane kaa ricard yusuf pathan ke naam he
 He is the second Indian batsman to score a century in the IPL
 unhone 2010 ke tisare sanskaran kaa pehla shatak mumbai indiens ke khilaaf lagaaya tha
 He completed 100 runs in just 37 balls with the help of nine fours and eight sixes
 is satr main pathan kaa balla bhi ab tak khamosh rahaa he
 Last year, in the fourth edition of the tournament, on the sixth day, Punjab opener Paul Walthatty scored an unbeaten century
 valthati ne chennai superkings ke khilaaf naabad 120 ran banaae the
 During this, he hit 19 fours and two sixes off 63 balls
 valthti bhi is satr main balle se kuch kamaal nahin kar sake hai
 The first century of the IPL is in the name of wicketkeeper batsman Brandon mccallum
 varsh 2008 main ipel ke udghaatan match ko bhala koun bhul saktaa he
 In the match played between the Royal Challengers Bangalore and the Knight Riders, mccallum rained fours and sixes in the very first match of the tournament, playing for the Knight Riders
 maiklam ne 73 gendon par 10 chaukon or 13 chhakkon kii madad se naabad 158 ran banaae the jo ipel main kisi bhi khilaadi dwaara banaaya gaya ab tak kaa ucch score he
 The match was won by the Knight Riders with a big margin of 140 runs
 ipel ke pehle sanskaran main chah shatak lage the to duusare main sirf do hi shatak lage
 The third edition took four centuries and then the fourth edition took six centuries
 pehle sanskaran main koi bhi bhartiya ballebaaj shatak nahin laga paaya tha to duusare main pandeya ne sirf shatak lagaaya
 The comments tisare sanskaran main pathan or murali vijay jaise bhartiya khilaadiyon ne shatak lagaae to chauthe sanskaran main sachin va sahvaag ne shatak jade
 Vijay is the third batsman after Rahane, Rohit among the Indian players to score a century this season
 is satr main jin teen videshi khilaadiyon ne shatak jade hai unamem kevin petersan, david warner or kris gail shaamil hai

 ipel kaa pehla shatak wicketiper ballebaaj brandan maiklam ke naam he
 Who can forget the opening match of IPL in 2008
 royal chalangers bangalore or niterides ke bich khele gaye mukaable main maiklam ne niterides kii ore se khelte hue toornament ke pehle hi match main chaukon or chhakkon kii barsaat kar di thi
 mccullum scored an unbeaten 158 off 73 balls with the help of 10 fours and 13 sixes, the highest score ever made by any player in the IPL
 is mukaable ko niterides ne 140 ranon ke bade antar se jeeta tha
 The first edition of the IPL took six centuries and the second took only two centuries
 tisare sanskaran main chaar shatak lage or phir chauthe sanskaran main chah shatak lage
 In the first edition, no Indian batsman could score a century, in the second, Pandey only scored a century
 tippaniyan Indian players like Pathan and Murali Vijay scored centuries in the third edition, while Sachin and Sehwag scored centuries in the fourth edition
 is satr main shatak lagane vaale bhartiya khilaadiyon main rahane, rohit ke baad vijay tisare ballebaaj hai
